# Otto — Nutrition breakdown (medium-confidence recipes)

Computed from USDA FoodData Central via Otto's real parser. Amounts estimated where the source omitted them, so every recipe returns a value. Guards applied: canned legumes→cooked, frying-oil→absorbed only. Flags: ✅ measured · 🟡 volume/density · 🟠 estimated.
